xl:layout:[--fd-toc-width:268px]"><h1 class="font-semibold mb-4 text-4xl tracking-tight">Mutation &amp; Revalidation</h1><div class="prose flex-1 mx-auto w-full"><p>SWR provides the <a class="font-normal text-primary no-underline" href="/en/docs/mutation#mutate"><code>mutate</code></a> and <a class="font-normal text-primary no-underline" href="/en/docs/mutation#useswrmutation"><code>useSWRMutation</code></a> APIs for mutating remote data and related cache.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="mutate"><a data-card="" href="#mutate" class="peer"><code>mutate</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>There&#x27;re 2 ways to use the <code>mutate</code> API to mutate the data, the global mutate API which can mutate any key and the bound mutate API which only can mutate the data of corresponding SWR hook.</p>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="global-mutate"><a data-card="" href="#global-mutate" class="peer">Global Mutate</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p>The recommended way to get the global mutator is to use the <a class="font-normal text-primary no-underline" href="/en/docs/global-configuration#access-to-global-configurations"><code>useSWRConfig</code></a> hook:</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { useSWRConfig } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;swr&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> App</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">mutate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> useSWRConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  mutate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(key, data, options)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>
<p>You can also import it globally:</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { mutate } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;swr&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> App</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  mutate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(key, data, options)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>
<div class="flex gap-2 my-4 border p-3 ps-1 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground rounded-sm bg-transparent p-3! shadow-none [&amp;_div[role=&#x27;none&#x27;]]:hidden" style="--callout-color:var(--color-fd-info, var(--color-fd-muted))" emoji="⚠️"><div role="none" class="w-0.5 bg-(--callout-color)/50 rounded-sm"></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-5 -me-0.5 fill-(--callout-color) text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="flex flex-col gap-2 min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin empty:hidden"><p>Using global mutator only with the <code>key</code> parameter will <em><strong>not update the cache or trigger revalidation</strong></em> unless there is a mounted SWR hook using the same key.</p></div></div></div>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="bound-mutate"><a data-card="" href="#bound-mutate" class="peer">Bound Mutate</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p>Bound mutate is the short path to mutate the current key with data. Which <code>key</code> is bounded to the <code>key</code> passing to <code>useSWR</code>, and receive the <code>data</code> as the first argument.</p>
<p>It is functionally equivalent to the global <code>mutate</code> function in the previous section but does not require the <code>key</code> parameter:</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> useSWR </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &#x27;swr&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Profile</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> () {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">data</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">mutate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> useSWR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;/api/user&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, fetcher)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">h1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;My name is {data.name}.&lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">h1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">button</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> onClick</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> () </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">        const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> newName</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> data.name.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toUpperCase</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">        // send a request to the API to update the data</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">        await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> requestUpdateUsername</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(newName)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">        // update the local data immediately and revalidate (refetch)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">        // NOTE: key is not required when using useSWR&#x27;s mutate as it&#x27;s pre-bound</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">        mutate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">...</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">data, name: newName })</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      }}&gt;Uppercase my name!&lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">button</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  )</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="revalidation"><a data-card="" href="#revalidation" class="peer">Revalidation</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p>When you call <code>mutate(key)</code> (or just <code>mutate()</code> with the bound mutate API) without any data, it will trigger a revalidation (mark the data as expired and trigger a refetch)
for the resource. This example shows how to automatically refetch the login info (e.g. inside <code>&lt;Profile/&gt;</code>)
when the user clicks the “Logout” button:</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> useSWR, { useSWRConfig } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &#x27;swr&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> App</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> () {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">mutate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> useSWRConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Profile</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">button</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> onClick</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{() </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">        // set the cookie as expired</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        document.cookie </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &#x27;token=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 UTC; path=/;&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">        // tell all SWRs with this key to revalidate</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">        mutate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;/api/user&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      }}&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        Logout</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">button</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  )</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>
<div class="flex gap-2 my-4 border p-3 ps-1 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground rounded-sm bg-transparent p-3! shadow-none [&amp;_div[role=&#x27;none&#x27;]]:hidden" style="--callout-color:var(--color-fd-info, var(--color-fd-muted))"><div role="none" class="w-0.5 bg-(--callout-color)/50 rounded-sm"></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-5 -me-0.5 fill-(--callout-color) text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="flex flex-col gap-2 min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin empty:hidden"><p>It broadcasts to SWR hooks under the same <a class="font-normal text-primary no-underline" href="/en/docs/advanced/cache">cache provider</a> scope. If no cache provider exists, it will broadcast to all SWR hooks.</p></div></div></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="api"><a data-card="" href="#api" class="peer">API</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="parameters"><a data-card="" href="#parameters" class="peer">Parameters</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<ul>
<li><code>key</code>: same as <code>useSWR</code>&#x27;s <code>key</code>, but a function behaves as <a class="font-normal text-primary no-underline" href="/en/docs/mutation#mutate-multiple-items">a filter function</a></li>
<li><code>data</code>: data to update the client cache, or an async function for the remote mutation</li>
<li><code>options</code>: accepts the following options<!-- -->
<ul>
<li><code>optimisticData</code>: data to immediately update the client cache, or a function that receives current data and returns the new client cache data, usually used in optimistic UI.</li>
<li><code>revalidate = true</code>: should the cache revalidate once the asynchronous update resolves. If set to a function, the function receives <code>data</code> and <code>key</code>.</li>
<li><code>populateCache = true</code>: should the result of the remote mutation be written to the cache, or a function that receives new result and current result as arguments and returns the mutation result.</li>
<li><code>rollbackOnError = true</code>: should the cache rollback if the remote mutation errors, or a function that receives the error thrown from fetcher as arguments and returns a boolean whether should rollback or not.</li>
<li><code>throwOnError = true</code>: should the mutate call throw the error when fails.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="return-values"><a data-card="" href="#return-values" class="peer">Return Values</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p><code>mutate</code> returns the results the <code>data</code> parameter has been resolved. The function passed to <code>mutate</code> will return an updated data which is used to update the corresponding cache value. If there is an error thrown while executing the function, the error will be thrown so it can be handled appropriately.</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">try</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> user</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> mutate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;/api/user&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">updateUser</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(newUser))</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">} </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">catch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (error) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // Handle an error while updating the user here</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="useswrmutation"><a data-card="" href="#useswrmutation" class="peer"><code>useSWRMutation</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>SWR also provides <code>useSWRMutation</code> as a hook for remote mutations. The remote mutations are only triggered manually, instead of automatically like <code>useSWR</code>.</p>
<p>Also, this hook doesn’t share states with other <code>useSWRMutation</code> hooks.</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> useSWRMutation </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &#x27;swr/mutation&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Fetcher implementation.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// The extra argument will be passed via the `arg` property of the 2nd parameter.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// In the example below, `arg` will be `&#x27;my_token&#x27;`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> updateUser</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">url</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">arg</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> }</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">arg</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> }) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> fetch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(url, {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    method: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;POST&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    headers: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      Authorization: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">`Bearer ${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">arg</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">}`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  })</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Profile</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // A useSWR + mutate like API, but it will not start the request automatically.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">trigger</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> useSWRMutation</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;/api/user&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, updateUser, options)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">button</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> onClick</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{() </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    // Trigger `updateUser` with a specific argument.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    trigger</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;my_token&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }}&gt;Update User&lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">button</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="useswrmutation-api"><a data-card="" href="#useswrmutation-api" class="peer">API</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="useswrmutation-parameters"><a data-card="" href="#useswrmutation-parameters" class="peer">Parameters</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<ul>
<li><code>key</code>: same as <a class="font-normal text-primary no-underline" href="/en/docs/mutation#mutate"><code>mutate</code></a>&#x27;s <code>key</code></li>
<li><code>fetcher(key, { arg })</code>: an async function for remote mutation</li>
<li><code>options</code>: an optional object with the following properties:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li><code>optimisticData</code>: same as <code>mutate</code>&#x27;s <code>optimisticData</code></li>
<li><code>revalidate = true</code>: same as <code>mutate</code>&#x27;s <code>revalidate</code></li>
<li><code>populateCache = false</code>: same as <code>mutate</code>&#x27;s <code>populateCache</code>, but the default is <code>false</code></li>
<li><code>rollbackOnError = true</code>: same as <code>mutate</code>&#x27;s <code>rollbackOnError</code></li>
<li><code>throwOnError = true</code>: same as <code>mutate</code>&#x27;s <code>throwOnError</code></li>
<li><code>onSuccess(data, key, config)</code>:　 callback function when a remote mutation has been finished successfully</li>
<li><code>onError(err, key, config)</code>: callback function when a remote mutation has returned an error</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="useswrmutation-return-values"><a data-card="" href="#useswrmutation-return-values" class="peer">Return Values</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<ul>
<li><code>data</code>: data for the given key returned from <code>fetcher</code></li>
<li><code>error</code>: error thrown by <code>fetcher</code> (or undefined)</li>
<li><code>trigger(arg, options)</code>: a function to trigger a remote mutation</li>
<li><code>reset</code>: a function to reset the state (<code>data</code>, <code>error</code>, <code>isMutating</code>)</li>
<li><code>isMutating</code>: if there&#x27;s an ongoing remote mutation</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="useswrmutation-basic-usage"><a data-card="" href="#useswrmutation-basic-usage" class="peer">Basic Usage</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> useSWRMutation </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &#x27;swr/mutation&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>

<p>If you want to use the mutation results in rendering, you can get them from the return values of <code>useSWRMutation</code>.</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">trigger</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">data</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">error</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> useSWRMutation</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;/api/user&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, sendRequest)</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2"
